  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_404183aa-481e-4b60-9908-715884c516cf'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };
    if (typeof AppleID !== "undefined") {
      initAppleId();
    } else {
      initializeSiwa();
    }

<span id="freeTextContainer4552416931151367986"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1472530620i/20203676.jpg' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1471374251ra/20039517.gif' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1472430374ra/20192768.gif' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1472442690ra/20193504.gif' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1472488577ra/20199588.gif' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1472495597ra/20200675.gif' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><b>★★★★★! El Diablo (stand-alone book 1). Meet the man behind the legend. Alejandro Martinez’s epic saga spanning decades!</b><br/><br/><a>

    <i>
      <b>“She was trying to save me when all I would do was destroy her.”</b>
    </i>
  </blockquote>
</a><br/>They called him <b>El Diablo,</b> the devil. <b>Alejandro Eduardo Martinez</b> spent his life running a worldwide mob empire. <br/><br/><b>Death and fortune</b> attached themselves to him. Governments bowed to him. The law bent for him. Men equally feared and admired him. And women swooned at his feet.<br/><br/><b>One woman</b> would come </span>

El Diablo (stand-alone book 1). Meet the man behind the legend. Alejandro Martinez’s epic saga spanning decades!</b><br><br><a>
  <blockquote>
    <i>
      <b>“She was trying to save me when all I would do was destroy her.”</b>
    </i>
  </blockquote>
</a><br>They called him <b>El Diablo,</b> the devil. <b>Alejandro Eduardo Martinez</b> spent his life running a worldwide mob empire. <br><br><b>Death and fortune</b> attached themselves to him. Governments bowed to him. The law bent for him. Men equally feared and admired him. And women swooned at his feet.<br><br><b>One woman</b> would come along. She would be <b>his weakness, his downfall and his salvation.</b> The man behind the legend. This is his epic saga, spanning decades. <br><br><a>
  <blockquote>
    <i>
      <b>“Little did she know, I was the villain in this story.”</b>
    </i>
  </blockquote>
</a><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1472530774ra/20203731.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Meet <b>Alejandro Eduardo Martinez</b>, the boy, the man, the gangster, the lover and… the legend!<br><br><b>The boy:</b> Once an innocent boy before love, betrayal, death and destruction wrecked any illusions of a normal life.<br><br><b>The man:</b> Violence, vengeance, jealousy and greed took every person who ever meant anything to him.<br><br><b>The gangster:</b> With nothing left to lose, he carried on and expanded his mob empire on the principles of ruthlessness and cunning.<br><br><b>The lover:</b> But one woman would bring him to his knees and she’d spend her life paying for it.<br><br><b>The legend:</b> He might have inherited the title El Diablo. But he became a legend in his own right!<br><br><a>
  <blockquote>
    <i>
      <b>“So here I am… What can my cock make you forget tonight?”</b>
    </i>
  </blockquote>
</a><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1472530774ra/20203732.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Nine words to describe <b>Lexi:</b> Innocent, broken, naïve, impressionable, unassuming, meek, steadfast, focused and survivor.<br><br><a>
  <blockquote>
    <i>
      <b>“Every devil needs an angel. And she was mine.”</b>
    </i>
  </blockquote>
</a><br><b>El Diablo,</b> told from dual POVs, in all its violence, death, destruction, betrayal, secrets and lies is the <b>perfect blend of intrigue, suspense, shockers and heartbreak.</b> It was a glued-to-your-Kindle addicting saga, with a bittersweet yet perfect ending!<br><br><b>I sob</b> for all the years wasted, lives lost, dreams crushed, hearts broken, but most of all for <b>the man caught behind the legend.</b> <i>Be still my beating heart.</i> <br><br>All-consuming! Unpredictable! Unforgettable! Epic! Kudos M. Robinson! <br><br><a>
  <blockquote>
    <i>
      <b>“You were the villain in your own story, Martinez. In mine, you’ve always been my hero.”</b>
    </i>
  </blockquote>
</a><br>***<br>Hero rating: 5+ stars <br>Heroine rating: 5 stars<br>Sexual tension rating: 5 stars<br>Sex scenes rating: 5 stars<br>Sex scenes frequency: 4.5 stars<br>Plot rating: 5+ stars<br>Dialogue rating: 5 stars<br>Storytelling rating: 5 stars<br>Story ending rating: 5 stars<br>**********************************************<br><b>Overall rating: 5 stars<br><br>Would I recommend this story: Yes.<br>Would I re-read this story: Yes.<br>Would I read future books by this author: Yes.</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1472512918ra/20202291.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Tagged along on shhlut’s (F)BR. <b>Thank you</b> Liz, LoLo, WaWa &amp; CC! <br><br><b>

The devil has truly left its mark as M. Robinson has cemented her place as an author that deserves your fu</span>
  <span id="freeText2989799638442322488" style="display:none"><i>ARC provided by author in exchange for an honest review</i><br><br><a href="http://s848.photobucket.com/user/msmeesh983/media/book%20reviews%20pics/Graphic%20Headline%20Titles%20Part%202/eb4a9cad8512793d79dfb68a5adcff_zpsmbo3hbaz.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1472512840i/20202283._SX540_.gif" alt=" photo eb4a9cad8512793d79dfb68a5adcff_zpsmbo3hbaz.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="http://s848.photobucket.com/user/msmeesh983/media/book%20reviews%20pics/Graphic%20Headline%20Titles%20Part%202/480707c743f9f5869f6f3125bfce8a_zpsrl62rxqo.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><b>She needed to stay away from me. I wanted her to stay away from me. I should've made her leave, but it didn’t matter because I couldn’t stay away from her any longer. And in the end…I didn’t want to.”</b><br><br>A seductive tantalizing read that will for sure leave readers <i>begging, wanting, craving, crying,</i> and <i>dying</i> for more of <b>El Diablo</b>!! The devil has truly left its mark as M. Robinson has cemented her place as an author that deserves your full undivided attention. Robinson delivers a sinful and calculating forbidden romance that will haunt and consume readers as hearts will ache, beg, be broken and slowly mended in M.Robinson’s angsty signature. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1472513164ra/20202297.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>The Devil.</i>
</b> I am not talking about the devil that lives in Hell but I’m talking about the devil that grins and who can seduce you with his bewitching tongue and destroy you with the snap of his fingers. That’s right. I am talking about Alejandro Martinez, aka <i>
  <b>El Diablo.</b>
</i><br><br><a href="http://s848.photobucket.com/user/msmeesh983/media/book%20reviews%20pics/Graphic%20Headline%20Titles%20Part%202/480707c743f9f5869f6f3125bfce8a_zpsrl62rxqo.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1472513503i/20202319.gif" alt=" photo 480707c743f9f5869f6f3125bfce8a_zpsrl62rxqo.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><b>Don't knock on the devil's door, sweetheart, and expect him not to answer. ”</b><br><br>If you have read M. Robinson’s previous book, <i>Crave Me,</i> you have already been introduced to the fucking devil himself but if you haven’t read that book, do not worry as <b>El Diablo</b> can be read as a standalone but I do not advise it since you will be missing out on details from the previous book but not that much. <br><br><a href="https://www.flickr.com/gp/66034700@N08/8faxfh" title="##ElDiablo1" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1472270535i/20174144.jpg" width="500" height="500" alt="##ElDiablo1" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Alejandro Martinez is as cunning and ruthless as they come. He is a sinner. A killer. A liar. An opportunist. To state he is a Machiavellian is an understatement, because this devil is unscrupulous and crafty. He is the snake in the grass waiting to make his deadly bite. Alejandro Martinez is insidious. Duplicitous. Deadly. Canny. He is <b>El Diablo.</b><br><br><a href="http://s848.photobucket.com/user/msmeesh983/media/book%20reviews%20pics/Graphic%20Headline%20Titles%20Part%202/480707c743f9f5869f6f3125bfce8a_zpsrl62rxqo.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1472513503i/20202319.gif" alt=" photo 480707c743f9f5869f6f3125bfce8a_zpsrl62rxqo.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><b>Saying sorry was a sign of weakness, and I couldn’t bring myself to say the two words. To show her that I had a weak side, buried under all the bullshit. I really wanted to beg for her forgiveness, over and over again for what I’d done.”</b><br><br>When it comes to Alejandro everything is a game. He is the mastermind that is pulling all the strings. He is the King and he rules with an iron hand. But this brutal and deadly sinner didn’t begin this way until he knew first hand that power is key. Power is the only way to control and have your enemies fear you. Power is the only way to protect your heart that is until she entered the picture……<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1464290011ra/19223824.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Lexi knows pain, loss, death, sacrifices, and monsters. Her life was never the picture perfect white picket fence that every girl dreams about. Instead, her life was about survival. Surviving to make ends meet and surviving to make her dreams of becoming a ballerina a reality. Hope was her grace and miracles don’t happen to girls like Lexi that is until she comes face to face with the devil himself.<br><br><a href="http://s848.photobucket.com/user/msmeesh983/media/book%20reviews%20pics/Graphic%20Headline%20Titles%20Part%202/480707c743f9f5869f6f3125bfce8a_zpsrl62rxqo.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1472513503i/20202319.gif" alt=" photo 480707c743f9f5869f6f3125bfce8a_zpsrl62rxqo.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><b>I loved her with every breath in my body, every piece of my fucked up heart, every last part of me belonged to her.”</b><br><br>Lexi is the forbidden fruit that Alejandro wanted to taste. She was the epitome of salvation, hope and possibly love. As much as he tried to resist and stay away from her, he couldn’t. She was a siren luring him with her innocence, beauty, and fierce personality. She is the only person who can look the devil in the eyes and not back down. And that alone was enough justification for Alejandro to corrupt Lexi sexually, physically, spiritually, and mentally. She was his instrument to play. And boy oh boy, did he play with her.<br><br><a href="https://www.flickr.com/gp/66034700@N08/0HeT3k" title="#ElDiablo2" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1472515712i/20202503.jpg" width="500" height="419" alt="#ElDiablo2" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="http://s848.photobucket.com/user/msmeesh983/media/book%20reviews%20pics/Graphic%20Headline%20Titles%20Part%202/480707c743f9f5869f6f3125bfce8a_zpsrl62rxqo.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1472513503i/20202319.gif" alt=" photo 480707c743f9f5869f6f3125bfce8a_zpsrl62rxqo.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><b>I had killed. I had avenged. I had loved. I had destroyed lives and now it was my time to pay for being the Grim fucking Reaaper, taking lives that didn't belong to me. I just never thought my life would end like this. ”</b><br><br>As Lexi and Alejandro dances around their feelings for one another, an unraveling of secrets begins to take place. Every lies and sins are exposed. The truth was begging to be told. And how far will the Devil go to protect his secrets? And the answer is simple, he will go to hell and back.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1472512840ra/20202284.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><a href="http://s848.photobucket.com/user/msmeesh983/media/book%20reviews%20pics/Graphic%20Headline%20Titles%20Part%202/480707c743f9f5869f6f3125bfce8a_zpsrl62rxqo.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1472513503i/20202319.gif" alt=" photo 480707c743f9f5869f6f3125bfce8a_zpsrl62rxqo.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><b>Every Devil needs an Angel. And she was mine.”</b><br><br><b>El Diablo</b> is by far the best book that M. Robinson has written to date. She took her writing to another level as she seductively weaves every facets of raw emotions to create a symphony of drama, angst, fourberie, betrayal, love, sacrifice, and unyielding passion. Robinson boldly paints a literary masterpiece where readers are taken down the proverbial rabbit hole where there is only way out and that is through the eyes of Alejandro Martinez. Every action has consequence. Every lie has a truth. And every pain has a reason. And so I urge, no beg you to read this cunning romance that will have you begging for more. And just remember The Devil was once an angel so discover why Alejandro Martinez is <i>the devil in the suit that grins. </i><br><br><a href="http://s848.photobucket.com/user/msmeesh983/media/book%20reviews%20pics/Graphic%20Headline%20Titles%20Part%202/f31fc5db1894686c3bbd2ddb1e89fb_zpshxmzlfrh.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

<div id="review_1741806523" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1741806523" />
    <a title="Candace" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/16384209-candace"><img alt="Candace" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1459720769p2/16384209.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1741806523?book_show_action=true">Aug 28, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Candace" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Candace" href="/user/show/16384209-candace">Candace</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=age-difference">age-difference</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=hate-that-i-love-them">hate-that-i-love-them</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=pregnant-heroines">pregnant-heroines</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=dangerous-hero-themed-books-read">dangerous-hero-themed-books-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=rich-guys">rich-guys</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=shocking-twists">shocking-twists</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=organized-crime">organized-crime</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1741806523" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17570511971206309501">Spanning decades, 'El Diablo' tells the story of Alejandro Martinez, a notorious cartel leader. Following him from his childhood, this book provides a front-row seat to the tragedy that was his life. He was born into the life and groomed from a young age to take over his father's role as leader of the cartel. In so many ways, he never stood a chance at a normal life.<br/><br/>Surviving the loss of numerous loved ones, especially the women closest to him, he grows into a callous man. He shows no emotion or</span>
  <span id="freeText17570511971206309501" style="display:none">Spanning decades, 'El Diablo' tells the story of Alejandro Martinez, a notorious cartel leader. Following him from his childhood, this book provides a front-row seat to the tragedy that was his life. He was born into the life and groomed from a young age to take over his father's role as leader of the cartel. In so many ways, he never stood a chance at a normal life.<br /><br />Surviving the loss of numerous loved ones, especially the women closest to him, he grows into a callous man. He shows no emotion or concern for others, afraid that his feelings are weaknesses that his enemies will exploit. He has earned his reputation as a ruthless crime lord, aptly called "El Diablo" on the streets.<br /><br />Lexi grows up without the love of parents. She's never known her real father and her other is emotionally absent on her best day. From a young age, she got used to taking care of herself. Being alone was the norm for her. <br /><br />When Lexi's circumstances go from bad to worse, she throws herself into her dance. Ballet was her only escape. Her only dream was to become a ballerina.<br /><br />Together, Alejandro and Lexi have incredible chemistry. The sexual tension and anticipation was incredible between these two. They played a back and forth game, literally for years. Every time I thought they were getting somewhere, Alejandro would do something to push Lexi away again. He definitely gave me some serious whiplash with his push and pull routine.<br /><br />In fact, I had a really hard time with Alejandro's cruel and contradictory behaviors. He was a world-class a$$hole for the vast majority of the book. The few times when he wasn't, were quickly followed-up by more reprehensible behavior on his part. I love an antihero, but Alejandro took the cake.<br /><br />That being said, I have a weakness for jerks (fictional characters only). If you don't, then you'll probably hate this book. Be forewarned--Alejandro is an a$$hat of epic proportions. He flaunts other women I front of Lexi, demeans her and says awful things. He was outright cruel often times.<br /><br />At the same time, I couldn't hate him. He spent years protecting Lexi and providing for her financially. Despite his emotionally closed-off demeanor, it was apparent that he cared for her in his own screwed up way. I definitely had a love/hate relationship with Alejandro.<br /><br />Even though this book did seem to go on for long periods of time without any remarkable events, I couldn't pull myself away from it. Talk about a slow-burn. It took years for these two to make it to third base! It might have even been a full decade before they had sex! Yet, I was completely absorbed in this story.<br /><br />There is a huge twist at the end, which will blow your mind. The big reveal was something that had crossed my mind early-on, but that I had dismissed as I got further into the story. Even though I had guessed part of the secret, I was still thrown for a loop and left shell-shocked when everything was finally aired. I was crushed.<br /><br />This book gutted me. I wanted to yell, cry and smash things! From beginning to end, I felt like I was on an emotional rollercoaster. I was afraid to find out what would jump out around the next bend, but to curious to look away. I loved it!<br /><br />Why then did I give it only 4 stars and not 5? I struggled with this one, but ultimately I decided to go with 4 stars because I thought that Lexi let Alejandro off easy. I expect my heroes to have to grovel and really work for forgiveness when they screw up...and Alejandro screwed up BIG on more than one occasion. Maybe it's my sadistic tendencies, but my inner bitch demanded blood! I wanted him to pay for what he put Lexi through. An apology and an explanation in a few pages didn't cover it after what he did. I wanted him to suffer some more.<br /><br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="17570511971206309501" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1688456284" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1688456284" />
    <a title="Christy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11284813-christy"><img alt="Christy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1594293998p2/11284813.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1688456284?book_show_action=true">Jul 05, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christy" href="/user/show/11284813-christy">Christy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1688456284" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18003968054696333881"><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%209/B10D5D11-F852-4188-B165-C525A9D9E169_zpsohwl6dnp.png.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1472601490i/20214160._SX540_.png' alt=' photo B10D5D11-F852-4188-B165-C525A9D9E169_zpsohwl6dnp.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><i>El Diablo</i> is another extremely angsty read from M. Robinson. This is one author who knows how to write an angsty story. It was an unexpected and thrilling ride with a great antihero. Martinez is one of those characters you will hate to love and love to hate. I love characters like this! <br/><br/><i>El Diablo</i> is Alejandro Martinez’s life story in a way. It spans decades and tells the story of a man who is the devil. At times, he is a monster, but he’s only the monster they created him to be. He’s not all</span>
  <span id="freeText18003968054696333881" style="display:none"><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%209/B10D5D11-F852-4188-B165-C525A9D9E169_zpsohwl6dnp.png.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1472601490i/20214160._SX540_.png" alt=" photo B10D5D11-F852-4188-B165-C525A9D9E169_zpsohwl6dnp.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><i>El Diablo</i> is another extremely angsty read from M. Robinson. This is one author who knows how to write an angsty story. It was an unexpected and thrilling ride with a great antihero. Martinez is one of those characters you will hate to love and love to hate. I love characters like this! <br><br><i>El Diablo</i> is Alejandro Martinez’s life story in a way. It spans decades and tells the story of a man who is the devil. At times, he is a monster, but he’s only the monster they created him to be. He’s not all bad, in fact he’s very attractive, cunning and captivating. Martinez never had a truly normal life. He grew up knowing one day he would follow in his father’s footsteps as the leader of the cartel. To do that, there would be no distractions. Not even the girl that he once loved… without love, he became El Diablo. The devil. The guy you were made to fear. <br><br>As Lexi grew up, all she wanted to be was a dancer. It was her dream. She would do anything to make that happen. Lexi’s life has been about surviving. If she wanted to make her dreams come true, she was going to do something about it. She’s a fiercely strong heroine who endures a lot in her life. <br><br>Lexi and Martinez skate around their feelings for some time. There is a lot between them. So many secrets. Martinez wants to protect her. As I said before, Martinez is one of those characters you love to hate and hate to love, but seeing those moments where you just know how much he truly cares for Lexi, it makes you love him. Even if you hate a lot of the choices he’s made throughout the story. <br><br>This is probably M. Robinson’s wildest ride yet. She writes some crazy stuff sometimes, and this one took the cake. It was full of secrets, violence, twists and turns. It’s one of those stories that will keep you guessing and you’ll be addicted to the angst in this story. This is loosely connected to the last book in The Good Ol’ Boys series, but can most definitely be read as a stand alone. If you’re looking for an intense and angst filled story with a fabulous anti-hero, this is one I recommend. </span>
  <a data-text-id="18003968054696333881" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer15837121185001804343"><i>5 My Dark Angel stars</i><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1472860726i/20329658._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/> <br/>The Devil is in the details, and this doesn't miss a thing... riding that fine line between <i>love</i> and <i>hate</i>. <br/><br/><b>Alejandro Martinez</b> is <i>
  <b>El Diablo</b>
</i><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>I had killed. I had avenged. I had loved. I had destroyed lives and now it was my time to pay for being the Grim fucking Reaper, taking lives that didn’t belong to me. </i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1472860726i/20329659.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>He's never wanted anything until he sees her, knowing all too painfully he can never let her near. After all nothing ever good comes to those that loved him</span>
  <span id="freeText15837121185001804343" style="display:none"><i>5 My Dark Angel stars</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1472860726i/20329658._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br> <br>The Devil is in the details, and this doesn't miss a thing... riding that fine line between <i>love</i> and <i>hate</i>. <br><br><b>Alejandro Martinez</b> is <i>
  <b>El Diablo</b>
</i><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>I had killed. I had avenged. I had loved. I had destroyed lives and now it was my time to pay for being the Grim fucking Reaper, taking lives that didn’t belong to me. </i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1472860726i/20329659.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>He's never wanted anything until he sees her, knowing all too painfully he can never let her near. After all nothing ever good comes to those that loved him. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1472860726i/20329660.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And you'd think after the fucked up mess fate has thrown their way they would get their happily ever after, destiny decides to be a bitch and destroy it all...<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1472860726i/20329661._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>El Diablo</b> will break your heart, there is no sugar coating him and his assholic ways. He is a man whose soul is consumed by demons, too blind to see what a gift Lexi is in his own personal hell. His story will consume you and make you wish you could save a man like him. This is a story of a dead man walking and the woman who loved him above all reason ready to walk through the flames of hell if it meant being by his side. I was all over the board with my feelings for him and thankful that Lexi is who she is; young but wise beyond her years. While I was pissed with him, Lexi was the anchor to the story, holding her own in a world where most will crumble. <br><br>It was brutal, honest and full of angst; guaranteed to be a story you either are going to love or hate. I can't say much as it is a story that you have to come to your own conclusions. I highly recommend you give it a try, especially if you are like me and love them larger than life and oh so bad.<br><br><i>ARC kindly provided by the author, via *Sixty First Reads*, in exchange for an honest review.</i><br> <br>***Quotes above are taken from the version of the book I received and may differ from published edition.<br><br><i>Side Note: This man is the PERFECT fantasy and doesn't this picture just melt your heart even more.</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1472861238i/20329821.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br></span>

        <a title="Jennifer Kyle" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jennifer Kyle" href="/user/show/9916227-jennifer-kyle">Jennifer Kyle</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9916227-jennifer-kyle?shelf=i-like-it-dark-and-twisted">i-like-it-dark-and-twisted</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1740308128" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11929032602597917829"><b>3.5 STARS</b><br/><br/><span>[image error]</span><br/><br/>The first forty percent of this story which spans the hero’s childhood to adulthood was definitely a five star read. Thereafter, I had a hard time with the manner in which the story was drawn out and dragged out till the reveals. I think for me, the first forty as a standalone story or prequel would have worked since I would have been prepared to let go of a heroine and embrace the hero’s new infatuation/love interest. Or perhaps if the story was just condensed a bunch in t</span>
  <span id="freeText11929032602597917829" style="display:none"><b>3.5 STARS</b><br><br><span>[image error]</span><br><br>The first forty percent of this story which spans the hero’s childhood to adulthood was definitely a five star read. Thereafter, I had a hard time with the manner in which the story was drawn out and dragged out till the reveals. I think for me, the first forty as a standalone story or prequel would have worked since I would have been prepared to let go of a heroine and embrace the hero’s new infatuation/love interest. Or perhaps if the story was just condensed a bunch in the second half?<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1492230762ra/22495820.gif" width="430" height="150" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>M. Robinson opens this story with a bang and I was completely connected to this crime family who suffers so many losses. The story spans decades as a young Alejandro Martinez is groomed to head this Columbian crime family and one day be known as EL DIABLO. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1571269976ra/28305425.gif" width="430" height="150" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><b>
  <i>”Even the Devil was an angel once, Alejandro. It’s only a matter of time until you become El Diablo, too.”</i>
</b><br><br>Once the story went into Alejandro’s reign I struggled with his love interest the lonely, poor, ballerina who may or may not be connected to him. <b>Shockingly there wasn’t any mob business involved in the whole book!</b> No connections, no meets, no deals, nada. It’s all the push and pull of Alejandro feelings for Lexi. He wants her yet he pushes her away, he’s her secret sugar daddy yet he can’t be with her… <br><br><b>
  <i>”She needed to stay away from me. I wanted her to stay away from me. I should’ve made her leave, but it didn’t matter because I couldn’t stay away from her any longer. And in the end…I didn’t fucking want to.”</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1492230762ra/22495822.gif" width="430" height="150" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Overall, the beginning truly packs a punch but what follows in the middle is a whole lot of nothing till the reveals. <br><br><b>
  <i>”You were the villain in your own story, Martinez. In mine, you’ve always been my hero.”</i>
</b><br></span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1738932113?book_show_action=true">Aug 25, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="NMmomof4" class="user" itemprop="url" name="NMmomof4" href="/user/show/24665574-nmmomof4">NMmomof4</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1738932113" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1404126562855233768"><b> 3 Stars</b><br/><br/><b>Overall Opinion: </b> Well, I honestly am struggling on how to rate this one. Many other readers are loving this book, including some of my GR friends, but I didn't love it. This is definitely NOT for my safety gals! I don't mind an "unsafe" book from time to time, so that wasn't my issue. I had some major issues with the pacing (see below section), the constant push/pull from the H, wanting the h to be stronger at the end, and there was an overall lack of some good grovel by the H. It kind </span>
  <span id="freeText1404126562855233768" style="display:none"><b> 3 Stars</b><br /><br /><b>Overall Opinion: </b> Well, I honestly am struggling on how to rate this one. Many other readers are loving this book, including some of my GR friends, but I didn't love it. This is definitely NOT for my safety gals! I don't mind an "unsafe" book from time to time, so that wasn't my issue. I had some major issues with the pacing (see below section), the constant push/pull from the H, wanting the h to be stronger at the end, and there was an overall lack of some good grovel by the H. It kind of lost me at the last push from the H, because both characters did things that I didn't feel were redeemed in the end. I was, however, satisfied with the ending for once! But, I felt like there was <i>a lot</i> of wasted time between the h and H that was unnecessary and maybe put in just for the sake of having some angst. It did keep me intruiged, and I did enjoy it at times...so I'm going with a middle of the road rating @ 3 stars.<br /><br /><b>Brief Summary of the Storyline: </b> I can't really break this down without ruining it, but I'd say that this is more Alejandro's story than Lexi's. We meet Alejandro as a young teen when his father is starting to have him learn the ways of his criminal empire. We see how his loved ones struggle with how he is changing, and he has some traumatic events happen that just further him into becoming the cruel, unfeeling man that he is later in life. We meet Lexi, who is many years younger than him, and they have an instant connection. Through many years, they keep on meeting and cannot deny that connection. There are some violent and sad moments, some hot sexy times, and some major angst going on...will they get a HEA?<br /><br /><b>POV:</b> This alternated between Lexi and Alejandro's POV.<br /><br /><b>Overall Pace of Story: </b> Ok. This was one of my biggest issues with the book. I feel like it is realistic in that relationships as complex as these ones do not happen over a few months, so I did appreciate that aspect. I think I was just bothered by the constant time jumps! This relationship between the h and H is told over what has to be 20 years! It took them way too long to get their shit together IMO. I just felt like it was a waste tbh. It took me a while to get into this book too. I wouldn't say it was slow, but the first section (it's broken down into 4) was about the H as a young man getting into the life and his relationship with his first love. While it was nice to have this insight, I felt like it just went on too long and I was ready to meet the h (which we don't until part 2). I skimmed a little in that first section, but no other times.<br /><br /><b>Instalove:</b> No. They take years to develop stronger feelings (but they do have a instant strong connection).<br /><br /><b>H rating:</b> 3 stars. Alejandro. Hmmm....what to say about him?! He was hot. He was cruel and scary. He was lonely and damaged. He was a pretty complex character...<br /><br /><b>h rating:</b> 3.5 stars. Lexi. I liked her attitude and how she gave sass to the H. She was a very strong character for the most part. I did want her to be stronger and make him grovel some more (especially towards the end) at times.<br /><br /><b>Sadness level: </b>Low/moderate. I teared up a few times, but I never needed any tissues.<br /><br /><b>Push/Pull:</b> Yes! <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ The H is constantly hot and cold. He pulls the h in and then pushes her away. This goes on up until the very end! They both pursue the relationship at times. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Heat level:</b> Moderate. They have some hot chemistry and scenes, but not so much that it takes away from the story.<br /><br /><b>Descriptive sex:</b> Yes <br /><br /><b>Safe sex:</b> Yes. Condoms are mentioned. The H had only gone without with his first love and the h, and I don't remember any mention of her practices with the OM.<br /><br /><b>OW/OM drama:</b> Yes, but not in the usual way <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[The whole 1st section is the H with OW as a young man (his first and only love other than the h). She breaks his heart. The h is almost engaged to OM during one of their separations <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[but he dies in car accident <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Sex scene with OW or OM:</b> Yes <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ There are more than a couple scenes with H and OW. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Cheating: </b>Not technically <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[They are recently separated (after being together for ~3 years straight), but the h walks in on him getting a bj by OW <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[that we later find out he did to push her away <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Separation:</b>Yes <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Many separations. It is implied that the h only had relations with one other man (during their 10 year separation), but I was under the impression that the H had other partners during all their separations. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Possible Triggers: </b>Yes <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Violence/killing, rape, loss of a parent, suicide, drug use by side character, child molestation, prostitution (side character), virgin h and manwhore H, and large age gap between h and H (20ish years?).  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Closure: </b> The events leading up to the ending are a little shocking, so I'm going to put this with a spoiler tag... <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[There was a great epilogue and HEA ending <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>How I got it:</b> I paid the $2.99 on Amazon.<br /><br /><b>Safety:</b> I'd call this <u>Not Safe</u> for most of the safety gals.<br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<br />- <b>Does Not</b> have cheating (technically, but see above "cheating" spoiler)<br />- <b>Does </b> have more than 1 descriptive sex scene with H and OW<br />- <b> Does</b> have the H pushing the h away<br />- <b> Does</b> have many separations between the h and H<br />- <b> Does </b> have abuse<br />- <b> Does Not</b> have OTT sad parts IMO (see "sadness" section above)<br />- <b>Does </b> have a HEA ending. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></span>

</a><br><br><b> EL DIABLO: </b> This kicks starts us off in the 'Prologue' yet again M.Robinson has cast her magic and I'm under her spell, the story grips you as soon as you start reading that very first page, as you progress further into it trepidation courses through your body.<br><br><b> PART 1: </b> From a young age Alejandro was groomed to take over the family business. We're introduced to fourteen year old Martinez, one of life's hardest lessons to be learnt having one of the most feared mob bosses as his father came to a head when he had to prove he was his father's son by conducting his first kill, execution style. All in the name of protecting ones he loves. <br><br><b>Age fifteen</b> <i> "I lost my virginity to a whore, all because my father was proud of me for murdering a man” </i><br><br><b>
  <i> “Protecting what’s mine without showing any weakness. Never backing down. It only took one wrong move in this life to end up with a bullet in your goddamn head.<br>Your enemies couldn’t hurt you if they didn’t know what you’re feeling. What you’re thinking.<br>It was the code of life.<br>A very thin fucking line between being dead, or alive.” </i>
</b><br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=2588mqa" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1472441432i/20193456._SY540_.jpg" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Chapter by chapter, we can see him getting dragged into the dark side of mob life more and more as his birthdays progress.<br><br>How far will one man go to protect the ones he loves? <br><br> <a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=3166glh" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1472416597i/20191623.png" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <i> My father had his dirty hands in everything from drugs to guns to clubs. <br>He was the definition of organized crime, and there was very little that he didn’t own and operate. Politicians, police, FBI agents, they were all corrupt and all in his pocket. <br>Not a damn thing could be traced back to him. <br>He’d built a motherfucking empire on nothing but shady-ass shit. </i><br><br>What was supposed to be a happy day of celebrations turned into a bloody massacre, a tinted out SUV headed right for them, rifles at the ready.<br><br><b>"NO!" I shouted with everything in me as the sound of shots ricocheted off metal and glass, ringing as screams echoed in the alley. <br>Bullets flying everywhere, decorating the car with holes. </b><br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=dxgr2o" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1472426653ra/20192524.gif" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Chapter twelve pushes us into the dark, gritty, emotional side of mob life at its worst. <b>"At that moment, I would have sold my soul to the Devil” </b> Martinez will never be the same from this point onwards, seeking revenge uppermost in his mind. <b> "My heart was never going to mend itself.” </b><br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=mcvo6t" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1472440452i/20193378._SY540_.jpg" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>This has definitely put me through the paces reading this, moments of pure rage, swooning, sadness, love, gasps, disbelief.<br><br><b> PART 2:</b> We're introduced to six year old Lexi, spoken in her own words, describing what life is like living within a household where she's neglected, a step father whose rarely at home and a mother that sleeps all day and into the night who never leaves the house.<br><br>The only time she's in her happy bubble is when she's ballet dancing, nothing can touch her.<br><br>Years go by with no change within the household, until everything changes. Left alone to be raised by her step father.<br><br><b>
  <i> “Now I'm alone with the monster almost daily.<br>Except I once used to call him…<br>My stepdad.” </i>
</b><br><br>When fifteen year old Lexi &amp; Martinez finally meet you get the feeling that she is going to be his undoing, she'll be the one that will bring him to his knees. He just doesn't know it yet!! <br><br><i>
  <b> “All little girls wanted a Prince Charming. <br>A knight in shining fucking armor.<br>Little did she know, I was the villain in this story.” </b>
</i><br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=2cwlso6" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1472448172i/20193957._SY540_.jpg" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Years go by until these two are re-acquainted, he may want to keep his distance from her but from afar he's always looking out for her, protecting her. He comes across so hard, cold, callous but now and then one of his layers gets chipped away and we see a glimpse of the young Martinez boy he used to be. <br><br><b> PART 3:</b> 5 Years Later <br><br>Killing a man in cold blood, to save her<br><br>Her protector <br>Her saviour <br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=3166glh" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1472416597i/20191623.png" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <i>“This was bad.<br>The blaze in her eyes.<br>The feel of her skin.<br>The smell of her scent all around me.<br>I. Was. Fucked.”</i><br><br>Martinez is a profoundly guarded man with layer upon layer, who lives a treacherous life filled with enemies from all quarters who will stop at nothing to see him ten feet under. As the years progressed he grew into a very powerful man, more so than his father ever was, never show weakness, never allow anyone close, never show love, he became known on the streets as <b>El Diablo.</b> <br><br><i>
  <b> "She needed to stay away from me. I wanted her to stay away from me. I should've made her leave, but it didn’t matter because I couldn’t stay away from her any longer. And in the end…I didn’t want to.” </b>
</i><br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=29z4kso" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1472446930i/20193915._SY540_.jpg" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>This author fast became one of my favourites and never disappoints. Highly recommend this book!!<br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=35in9kk" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1472323045i/20180765._SX540_.jpg" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1472446930i/20193916._SX540_.jpg" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br></span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1640224332?book_show_action=true">May 16, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="✰ Liz ✰ " class="user" itemprop="url" name="✰ Liz ✰ " href="/user/show/27276528-liz">✰ Liz ✰ </a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1640224332" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13955745771689836161"><b>~4.5 DEVIL STARS~</b><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"I knew I was going to Hell. I just never imagined...I would be taking her with me."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1473091092i/20406079.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>El Diablo</b> is a dark and delicious treat full of action, suspense, angst, intrigue, passion, and dark romance. The highly anticipated story of Alejandro the ruthless mob boss certainly does not disappoint! We met Alejandro in the final book of the Good Ol' Boy Series <b>Crave Me</b>. Although <b>El Diablo</b> can be read as a stand-alone, I was so happy to have read the entire Good Ol' Boy Series be</span>
  <span id="freeText13955745771689836161" style="display:none"><b>~4.5 DEVIL STARS~</b><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"I knew I was going to Hell. I just never imagined...I would be taking her with me."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1473091092i/20406079.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>El Diablo</b> is a dark and delicious treat full of action, suspense, angst, intrigue, passion, and dark romance. The highly anticipated story of Alejandro the ruthless mob boss certainly does not disappoint! We met Alejandro in the final book of the Good Ol' Boy Series <b>Crave Me</b>. Although <b>El Diablo</b> can be read as a stand-alone, I was so happy to have read the entire Good Ol' Boy Series because it gave me a full perspective on the arc of these characters!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1473091386i/20406134._SX540_.gif" width="" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"Actions will always speak louder than words."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote>Alejandro wasn't always "the devil". As a son, brother, and friend, he begins his coming of age just trying to learn how to be a man. Despite the tenderness and goodness in his mom, it doesn't take him long to be swept up into the family business. His domineering father takes hold of him and thrusts him deep into the darkness of the crime world. Despite his father's best efforts to keep Alejandro deeply entrenched in the dark, his son still manages to find love. He loves his sister passionately and falls in love with a sweet girl from the "wrong side of the tracks". Although he tries to protect them both from the evils surrounding them, there is nothing that can stop the evil to come! But even "the devil" deserves some goodness in his life, right?<blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"Contemplating if this was the life that I was destined to lead. No family. No love. No God. Only darkness.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1473091092i/20406080.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"She was like the forbidden fruit I wanted to fuck."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote>After losing his first love, years pass, and Alejandro continues to grow hard. The darkness continues to swallow him whole, and it seems that there is nothing that can pull him out. It is the bright eyes of a ballerina named Lexi that seem to spin his world off of its axis and causes him to grasp a glimmer of light. And yet, with so many secrets, missed opportunities, and gut-wrenching moments spent between the two it seems that maybe Alejandro will never be able to escape the dark. <blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"I was already going straight to fucking Hell. I just didn't want to drag her into the inferno with me."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1473091092i/20406081.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"Placing her leg back on the lowest barre. I eased into her opening from behind, stretching her slowly, gently, letting her adjust to my size. Rubbing her breasts, stimulating her clit at the same time. Playing her body like it was made just for me."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote>Told in dual POV, <b>El Diablo</b> spans several agonizing decades. As the plot unfolds, there were numerous twists and turns that left me shaking my head and clutching my Kindle for dear life. Alejandro's evolution was painful and full of heartbreak. I felt that his character development was explored quite expertly, and every aspect of that's man persona held me captive the entire read. Lexi was a perfect counterpart for Alejandro. I was quite impressed with her tenacity and spunky spirit. Together they share an explosive ride full of multiple moments of joy, passion, and gut-wrenching heartbreak. There was a point in the process that I was more than ready for a resolution! Needless to say, this is not a read for the faint of heart. There were certain shifts in the plot that were quite shocking and yet; I feel like M. Robinson is always 100% committed to seeing her characters through. The more pain these characters experience the sweeter the joy at the end of the journey. I thoroughly enjoy the writing style of this author and as always, the steam factor is off the chart. Although Alejandro is a mob man, it is imperative to note that the story's main focus is on the journey of Alejandro and his quest for allowing himself to be loved. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1473091386i/20406134._SX540_.gif" width="" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Overall, I cannot recommend <b>El Diablo</b> enough. With its addictive blend of sexy romance, action, intrigue, and dark undertones, it will keep you entertained the entire read. In true M. Robinson style, integrated into the story she offers a sliver of what is to come. With an MC Series in the works, no doubt there will be many more winning reads to come from the "Queen of Angst". When M. Robinson is writing, my Kindle is always ready and waiting!<br><br><b>*This is a BR with my SHHLUTTY SISTA'S CC, WAR, LOYDA, and SUEBEE!*<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1472416031i/20191594._SX540_.jpg" width="200" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>*ARC graciously provided via author in exchange for an honest review!*<br><br>For more reviews/reveals/giveaways visit:<br><a href="https://craziesrusbookblog.wordpress.com//" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1434387282i/15214674._SX540_.jpg" width="350" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img Don't get me wrong, he was scary as hell and had a huge price on his head but he had not always been this way. <br/><br/>I loved the way the story is told through his entire life. <br/>From the small sweet boy to the cruel man that he turned into.   <span id="freeText13529567509734856230" style="display:none"><b>5 beautifully broken and soulless stars for El Diablo!!<br><br>As much as I wanted to hate Alejandro Martinez, I couldn't do it. Don't get me wrong, he was scary as hell and had a huge price on his head but he had not always been this way. <br><br>I loved the way the story is told through his entire life. <br>From the small sweet boy to the cruel man that he turned into. It was at times hard to keep up with his age. I think he was in 50's by the end of the book? Either way, he was still rocking that hot body and having sex daily. Does that even happen in real life? Who knows!! <br><br>Alejandro was a good guy despite being the son of one of the meanest cartel leaders in the in New York. He loved his mother, sister and fiancé. He was happy and ready to marry the love of his life. He knew that one day he would take over the business but he thought that it would be years.<br><br><a href="http://s304.photobucket.com/user/dwoods5/media/6392689B-2EB7-4F98-B35A-C68AFB4C99F5_zps6mphm5rl.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1475157206i/20689506.jpg" alt=" photo 6392689B-2EB7-4F98-B35A-C68AFB4C99F5_zps6mphm5rl.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br>One tragic event changed everything for this beautiful man. The terrible things that happened were like a domino effect. With everything happening Alejandro died and El Diablo was born!!<br><br><a href="http://s304.photobucket.com/user/dwoods5/media/03AD90B0-49BB-4E2B-9DF0-BD69985254B4_zpseg3frgmb.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1475157206ra/20689507.gif" alt=" photo 03AD90B0-49BB-4E2B-9DF0-BD69985254B4_zpseg3frgmb.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br>El Diablo was a cruel and soulless devil. Everyone wanted a piece of the devil. He trusted no one and had very thin patience. He would shoot a mofo in the head quick if they pissed him off.<br><br>Lexi was the one person that could honest to God bring this man to his knees. He knew that and he fought it hard. He was so cruel to her and said such terrible things. No matter what though, she loved him. All she ever wanted was to be a ballerina and to be loved. Lexi knew that there was a good person deep inside. She wanted nothing more than to be the woman by his side and to be the woman in his bed every night. She loved him so much and he broke her spirit a little every day. It was sad to see what loving the devil for so many years did to her mentally. One minute he was so sweet and kind and the next he was pushing her away. <br><br><a href="http://s304.photobucket.com/user/dwoods5/media/AABC1BA5-06FB-464E-B557-3C01001916CF_zpslth2jidg.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1475157206ra/20689508.gif" alt=" photo AABC1BA5-06FB-464E-B557-3C01001916CF_zpslth2jidg.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br>As much as I wanted her to run far away from him, I also loved that she never give up on him. She was never afraid of Alejandro because she knew that he would never hurt her physically. <br><br>This craziness went on for years and years. <br><br>I absolutely recommend it but just know that it is in no way sweet. It is dark and cruel. If you are anything like me, you will probably scream, cry and throw your kindle down and walk away for a while. At the 90% mark, I was pretty sure that I was having a mild anxiety attack. The joys of getting lost in a book and stepping away from the real world for a while!!</b></span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">People who love crime bosses and long timeline stories</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25494927-warhawke?shelf=romance-love">romance-love</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25494927-warhawke?shelf=criminals">criminals</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1741211740" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5301194845848843610"><b>Genre: </b>Contemporary Romance<br/><b>Type: </b>Standalone Book 1 from El Diablo series<br/><b>POV: </b>First Person - Dual<br/><b>Rating: </b><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1454075031i/17913446.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1472612322i/20215332.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Alejandro Martinez grew up as a mob prince. As the son of the feared leader, he was groomed to take over the empire. But crime life quickly took its toll when the people he loved were taken away from him one by one. He earned the name El Diablo from being ruthless and heartless, locking his heart from emotion until a young girl wormed herself into his life.<br/><br/>Lexi learned to be independent since</span>
  <span id="freeText5301194845848843610" style="display:none"><b>Genre: </b>Contemporary Romance<br><b>Type: </b>Standalone Book 1 from El Diablo series<br><b>POV: </b>First Person - Dual<br><b>Rating: </b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1454075031i/17913446.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1472612322i/20215332.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Alejandro Martinez grew up as a mob prince. As the son of the feared leader, he was groomed to take over the empire. But crime life quickly took its toll when the people he loved were taken away from him one by one. He earned the name El Diablo from being ruthless and heartless, locking his heart from emotion until a young girl wormed herself into his life.<br><br>Lexi learned to be independent since a very young age. With a useless mother, she redirected her love to ballet instead. It became a passion that provided her with an escape from hard life. When an opportunity knocked, she needed help to make her dream come through and it took her to El Diablo's doorstep, never realizing how it would change her life.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1453882133i/17883711.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Martinez had a brief appearance in the last book of Good 'Ol Boys series, Crave Me. His persona as a mob boss was mysterious and intriguing, and made you want to know more about him. Now is his chance to shine and shine he did.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b> <i>I never apologized for who I was or my actions.</i></b>
</blockquote><br><br>Alejandro exuded power and influence since he was old enough to hold a gun. His father only ever gave tough love and that's how he lived his life as an adult. I'm aware a lot of people have the love/hate thing on him, but for me, I love him for being him. I guess because villains make my heart swell in pride hahaha!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1472612322i/20215333.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>I like how spunky and fiery Lexi was especially when she was much younger. She wasn't afraid to go head to head with The Devil. However, I did question some of the things she did - as in she accepted certain scenarios too easily considering how she was supposed to be headstrong.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b> <i>Even God wasn't safe from me. I was a ruthless motherfucker who didn’t take no for an answer. No one crossed me and lived to tell the tale. I had no respect or loyalty to anyone but myself.</i></b>
</blockquote><br><br>I've always love stories that spanned years because we can see the characters evolution as long as they stayed true to the essence of their personality. I appreciate that the book has a lot of things going on and how things were wrapped up, even though none of the revelations surprised me. <br><br>One thing I wish differently is for the story to have more "showing" than "telling". I am also not a fan of muddled POV - one character constantly interpreting the other characters words/actions/emotions. I rather see it from the other character's first person perspective.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b> <i>“Don’t knock on the devil’s door, sweetheart, and expect him not to answer.”</i></b>
</blockquote><br><br>El Diablo is a story of two individuals whose life crossed and took them into a journey of happiness and heartache. The storyline was wrapped up and primed for the next book in the series.<br><br><br><b>⚜ ♆ ⚜ . . . (F)BR With The Shhluts . . . ⚜ ♆ ⚜</b><br><i>Comprised of Javigina Twinsie CC, CryBaby Loyda, Lonestar Liz and Queen SuSu :D</i><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1453876994i/17883340.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>For more reviews/reveals/giveaways visit:</b><br><a href="http://warhawkevault.wordpress.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1454304059i/17942101.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a href="http://warhawkevault.wordpress.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1451029682i/17500808.png" width="40" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="https://www.facebook.com/WarhawkesVault" rel="nofollow noopener">

<span id="freeTextContainer15491363311980343980"><b>5 FANFUCKINTASTIC!!!!!!!!!!!!!!! Stars</b><br/><br/>OMG, I loved this book sooooooooooooooooo much. This is going to be a really hard review to write because...............<br/><a href='http://s989.photobucket.com/user/Alicia_Mackey/media/thefeels_zps5kz8msds.gif.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>

</a><br/><br/>This superbly written book had everything I love in a book, intrigue, drama, suspense, twists and a dark side all of its own. <br/><br/>This was not a mafia/mob or cartel book as I thought going into it, it was the story of one mans fate in life. It starts when he is 15 and finishes when his in his 50s, so you get to read all the life changing ev</span>
  <span id="freeText15491363311980343980" style="display:none"><b>5 FANFUCKINTASTIC!!!!!!!!!!!!!!! Stars</b><br><br>OMG, I loved this book sooooooooooooooooo much. This is going to be a really hard review to write because...............<br><a href="http://s989.photobucket.com/user/Alicia_Mackey/media/thefeels_zps5kz8msds.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1474952877ra/20660365.gif" alt=" photo thefeels_zps5kz8msds.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>This superbly written book had everything I love in a book, intrigue, drama, suspense, twists and a dark side all of its own. <br><br>This was not a mafia/mob or cartel book as I thought going into it, it was the story of one mans fate in life. It starts when he is 15 and finishes when his in his 50s, so you get to read all the life changing events that turn Alejandro into El Diablo (the devil). Some of these life changing events are caused by his choices but others are just plain heartbreaking. <br><a href="http://s989.photobucket.com/user/Alicia_Mackey/media/yourkillingmeman_zpsomjvmip3.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1474953084ra/20660386.gif" alt=" photo yourkillingmeman_zpsomjvmip3.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I was a little worried as the first 30% for me just seemed to drag and took a while to read, I can see how some people I know DNF. Now after reading the entire book the first 30% is really important to the story and the rest of the book I just did not want to put down. <br><br>I will not go into the characters much as that will give away the plot. I was sure I had parts of this sussed out but I was wrong thank god *LOL*. I will say that I loved Lexi, her strength and patience were amazing.<br><br>I like my books to have sex in them and the hotter the better but I was so lost in this story that I didn't mind the lack of action. I was getting a little worn down by the continual push and pull, will they or will they not it nearly had me pulling my hair out. When they finally do (properly) at 80% mind you, it was totally worth it and I think the wait even made it better.<br><br>So wrapping this messy review up I want to say that this book has left me satisfied in the best possible way and I would gladly recommend this book to anyone.<br><a href="http://s989.photobucket.com/user/Alicia_Mackey/media/totallywicked_zpsytdtkcgf.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1474953835ra/20660429.gif" alt=" photo totallywicked_zpsytdtkcgf.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer776450711916922552"><b>PLEASE NOTE THAT THERE ARE SPOILERS AHEAD</b><br/><br/>I am really struggling to write a review on this book.....<br/>Most of the readers of GR have loved El Diablo but for me.........it just didn't do it!!! There were more things I disliked about the whole book than I actually liked. <br/><br/>Now don't get me wrong....I don't mind reading "dark" stories and I was looking forward to finding out what all those 4/5 stars reviews were all about.<br/><br/>The first part of the book was okay....I felt for the trauma that the two main cha</span>
  <span id="freeText776450711916922552" style="display:none"><b>PLEASE NOTE THAT THERE ARE SPOILERS AHEAD</b><br /><br />I am really struggling to write a review on this book.....<br />Most of the readers of GR have loved El Diablo but for me.........it just didn't do it!!! There were more things I disliked about the whole book than I actually liked. <br /><br />Now don't get me wrong....I don't mind reading "dark" stories and I was looking forward to finding out what all those 4/5 stars reviews were all about.<br /><br />The first part of the book was okay....I felt for the trauma that the two main characters went through their childhood. But suddenly I began to get totally annoyed with everyone and everything.<br /><br /><b>What I hated the most :</b><br /><br />The hero, Alejandro is in his 40's and the heroine, Lexi is 24 years old. <br />The hero sleeps with both mother and daughter!!!!<br />I absolutely detested the manner in which Alejandro treated Lexi.........he has sex with another woman knowing that Lexi can hear the sounds....and he professes that he loves Lexi!!!! PLEASE!!!! <blockquote>
  <b>“The fact that I caused Lexi pain, when in reality all I wanted to do was to provide her with comfort.”</b>
</blockquote>How sick is this guy!!!!<br />Alejandro treats Lexi without respect - he stalks her....he messes with her head....he's totally disgusting!!! I HATED THE F@@@@@@@$###.........And he never changes the way he's towards her....what the hell does Lexi want with someone like him!!!!!<br /><br />I did, however, like Lexi....in fact, she was the only character I had any feelings for. She was strong and I liked her sassy attitude...but I just so wished she would have made Alejandro grovel and bow.....but no!!!<br /><br />Anyway, to end off my ranting and raving - for me....it was just under an ok read...all because of Lexi............</span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
