<span id="freeTextContainer14375194502435421323"><b>*****4.5 STARS*****</b><br/>For my unfiltered review... <a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='https://prettymessreading.wordpress.com/2017/01/19/yasssss-%F0%9F%99%8C%F0%9F%8F%BE-el-diablo-by-m-robinson/'>https://prettymessreading.wordpress.c...</a><br/><br/>Let me take the time to introduce my future baby daddy… Alejandro Martinez aka El Diablo (The Devil). I am aware that commits murders in his spare time but that doesn’t stop my love for him, if anything, it me love him more.<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1484943706i/21770461._SY540_.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Let me start by saying that M. Robinson did an amazing job at building the characters in this book. I don’t know how she did it, but she did. So, bravo!!!<br/><br/>Before Martinez became El Diablo, h</span>
  <span id="freeText14375194502435421323" style="display:none"><b>*****4.5 STARS*****</b><br>For my unfiltered review... <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://prettymessreading.wordpress.com/2017/01/19/yasssss-%F0%9F%99%8C%F0%9F%8F%BE-el-diablo-by-m-robinson/">https://prettymessreading.wordpress.c...</a><br><br>Let me take the time to introduce my future baby daddy… Alejandro Martinez aka El Diablo (The Devil). I am aware that commits murders in his spare time but that doesn’t stop my love for him, if anything, it me love him more.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1484943706i/21770461._SY540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Let me start by saying that M. Robinson did an amazing job at building the characters in this book. I don’t know how she did it, but she did. So, bravo!!!<br><br>Before Martinez became El Diablo, he was Alejandro Martinez, son of one of the most notorious crime bosses on the east coast. His father was also the devil but over the years Alejandro would become more ruthless than his father.<br><br>Years of violence, drugs, whores and more turned Alejandro into the devil himself. He didn’t completely mind becoming the devil, he just didn’t want to take his first love with him, Sophia.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>See, I also knew I was going to Hell.<br><br>I just never imagined…<br><br>I would be taking her with me. – Martinez</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br>Sophia was everything he ever wanted, she was to be his wife. She was to like his mother. The big question was, could Sophia be a ride or die type female like his mother? Even his father questioned if Sophia was about that life.<br><br><i>“Do you think she’s strong enough to handle our lifestyle? Your future?”</i><br><br>There was something I found beautiful about Sophia but I never got the vibe that she was for him. I don’t know why, but I just didn’t. I wanted to. Over time Alejandro’s dad came to accept their relationship and eventually their engagement. Sophia loved that his father opened up to the idea of him and even began to like his father as a person, stupid girl.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“Look at me,” I ordered in a harsh tone. “He’s the Devil, Sophia. He’s the goddamn Devil. I never want you thinking he’s anything but.”<br><br>“And you? What does that make you?”<br><br>“Next in line,” I replied without hesitation.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br>But Alejandro wasn’t feeling that. He needed Sophia to know that his father was a horrible and one day he would be too.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Are you going to change when you take over?”<br><br>“You shouldn’t ask questions you really don’t want the answers to. I am who I am, Sophia.”<br><br>“Have you killed anyone else?”<br><br>“What I do is none of your concern.”<br><br>“So that’s a yes.”<br><br>“It’s not a no.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>Sophia should have know what she was getting into considering she was present the first time Alejandro killed a man. But some women are just stupid and she fell into that category. At the end of the book we find out just how stupid she really was.<br><br>When Sophia abandons Alejandro when he needs her the most, that’s when shit really hits the fan. Alejandro disappears and El Diablo is truly born. But you know what? El Diablo is 10 times sexier that Alejandro and Alejandro was pretty damn fine! So yeah, that devil could have me anyway he wanted.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1464290011ra/19223824.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>So this is the point where we stop discussing weak bitches and bring in a true “ride or die” female, Miss Lexi herself. Don’t get me wrong, at times Lexi is just as stupid as Sophia but in a completely different way. Lexi’s vice was her unwavering love for Martinez, that love would eventually turn her world inside out. What’s worse is that she took the emotional pain he caused her for over 10+ years.<br><br>I’m going to tell you right now, there is no way in hell I would ever wait for someone to give me their all for over 10+ years. Fuck that. You get 2 years max and that’s with me being generous, very generous. You better have some bomb ass sex for me to even consider waiting.<br><br>From what I read, Martinez could put it down in that department. I might have given him 3 years.<br><br>Good God Almighty!<br><br>Martinez and Lexi’s love story was H.O.T. hot! Pure fire!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1484943706i/21770462._SY540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>By the time Lexi comes into the picture, Martinez was already one of the most feared men on the east coast. His ties to the underground world earned him the name, El Diablo and for good fucking reason.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>Even God wasn’t safe from me. I was a ruthless motherfucker who didn’t take no for an answer. No one crossed me and lived to tell the tale. I had no respect or loyalty to anyone but myself – El Diablo</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>You didn’t want to cross this man.<br><br>Even the devil had family and Martinez was no different. He family was his weakness, one he tried to protect by keeping them away from him but even that wasn’t enough. Martinez would eventually have to bring his family in closer than he ever wanted. He had to raise his niece. But even that had it’s boundaries and limitations.<br><br>Although he had to raise his niece, he refused to allow her to love him. He wouldn’t even give the little girl a hug. He was turning into a father that resembled his own, cold and empty. He was unable to show his niece love so she wouldn’t love him back. But he loved the shit out of her.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>…it was easier for her to see me as a monster. I never wanted her to love me. I didn’t deserve it. <br><br>She didn’t deserve it.<br><br>The two women who loved me the most were both six feet under. There was no way in hell I would provoke fate again. – Martinez</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>I can’t say I blame him for keeping his niece, Briggs at arms length but it was difficult to read about. I hurt for him and hurt even more for Briggs. Everyone needs a family to love and neither of them had that anymore.<br><br>It was so sad. Oh, the feels.<br><br>I guess that what happens when your raised with a father like Martinez’s. His father was one fucked up individual. I mean he was proud of his son just for murdering a man.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1484869033i/21762559._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>I spent the rest of the night fucking her in every possible position known to man. i lost my virginity to a whore, all because my father was proud of me for murdering a man. If that wasn’t fucked up…<br><br>Then I don’t know what is. – Martinez</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br>But Lexi saw past El Diablo, she was able to see Alejandro, the man inside. She was willing to fight for this man, a man that she felt so connected to. She stood by his side even when he didn’t realize it. Crazy thing was… he was always by her side. (You’re going to have to read the book to see what I’m talking about.)<br><br>“As much as I tried to show you my Hell, you were more than willing to burn right along with me.” – Martinez<br>Lexi became Martinez’s secret obsession, which was dangerous for a man like him. If anyone know how he really felt about her, he knew they would use her to get what they wanted from him. He wasn’t having that. So, he had to keep his feelings in check. OMG, did he. He was one disciplined man, that’s for damn sure.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>She needed to stay away from me. That was the right thing to do. I was no good for her.<br><br>She looked at me as a savior, her hero, when I was anything but those things. – Martinez</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br>But El Diablo didn’t work that way.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>Saying sorry was a sign of weakness, and I couldn’t bring myself to say the tow words. To show her that I had a weak side, buried under all the bullshit. I really wanted to beg for her forgiveness, over and over again for what I’d done. Not just for tonight but all the other times she mentioned. But in the end, I was who I was, not even Lexi could change that.<br><br>I just wasn’t made that way. – El Diablo</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>There are so many twists and turns in this book, it’s crazy! I loved every bit of it!<br><br><br><br><br>Follow all my crazy….<br>Instagram <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.instagram.com/prettymessreading/">https://www.instagram.com/prettymessr...</a><br><br>Facebook <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.facebook.com/prettymessreading/">https://www.facebook.com/prettymessre...</a><br><br>Twitter <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://twitter.com/prettymessread">https://twitter.com/prettymessread</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="14375194502435421323" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<span id="freeTextContainer17851318556279536699"><b>5 Sinful Stars*****</b><br/><br/><i>(ARC kindly provided by author in exchange for an honest review)</i> <br/><br/>Author M. Robinson; the undisputed queen of angst is back with another heart pounding novel, that will claim your heart from the moment you read the prologue. <i>El Diablo</i> will set your heart on fire, he will own you, hurt you, and love you like no other... <br/><br/><a href='http://s1366.photobucket.com/user/DVFmontoya/media/Mobile%20Uploads/AB230774-6FBB-4178-B513-8BF15FAF8BE8_zps7cuivxnp.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1472422366i/20192201._SY540_.jpg' alt=' photo AB230774-6FBB-4178-B513-8BF15FAF8BE8_zps7cuivxnp.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Alejandro Martinez is the heir of a powerful Colombian drug cartel. From a young age he was being molded into becoming the ruthless leader that would follow </span>
  <span id="freeText17851318556279536699" style="display:none"><b>5 Sinful Stars*****</b><br><br><i>(ARC kindly provided by author in exchange for an honest review)</i> <br><br>Author M. Robinson; the undisputed queen of angst is back with another heart pounding novel, that will claim your heart from the moment you read the prologue. <i>El Diablo</i> will set your heart on fire, he will own you, hurt you, and love you like no other... <br><br><a href="http://s1366.photobucket.com/user/DVFmontoya/media/Mobile%20Uploads/AB230774-6FBB-4178-B513-8BF15FAF8BE8_zps7cuivxnp.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1472422366i/20192201._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo AB230774-6FBB-4178-B513-8BF15FAF8BE8_zps7cuivxnp.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Alejandro Martinez is the heir of a powerful Colombian drug cartel. From a young age he was being molded into becoming the ruthless leader that would follow into his father's footsteps. For The Martinez men, family is everything, they would do anything to protect their own, and the family's honor. <br><br>From a young age he had to accept that he could never have a normal life. He was forced into a dark and gritty world where respect was earn with blood. His ruthless nature made him push the envelope, creating destruction around those who would dare to cross him, becoming a dangerous man everybody feared, and gaining the name, <i>El Diablo</i>, which means The Devil.<br><br>Lexi grew up in a home where her mom was trapped inside her house due to an acute depression, and a stepfather who was always away working. All Lexie aver dreamed about was dancing, and for her mom to wake up one day, and not be sad anymore. But life had other plans for her, she would discover pain and disappointment from a very young age. Lexie had to create an armor, a tough and sassy exterior to protect herself from the outside world. Dancing became everything to her after her world crumbled. <br><br>Lexie met the man people call El Diablo when she was just a kid, and even though she was intimidated by him she never let it show. Years later when she needed help to accomplish her dream, she went straight to the gates of hell looking for the only person who could help her, <i>El Diablo.</i><br><br><a href="http://s1366.photobucket.com/user/DVFmontoya/media/Mobile%20Uploads/0F1126DF-2F1E-44C1-8304-D9351C63CBB3_zpsmcudceyu.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1472422366i/20192202._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 0F1126DF-2F1E-44C1-8304-D9351C63CBB3_zpsmcudceyu.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Years later Lexie is living her dream of dancing in a well renowned company, when trouble comes knocking on her door once again, and Martinez is the dark knight who saves her.<br><br>Alejandro is in charge of protecting Lexie. He has to fight with everything he has not to sin with the sexy woman who he's known for years, and is suddenly now sleeping in the room next to his. Is not an easy task for him, she's blossomed into a sensual woman, and every time she dances to the rhythm of music, he's mesmerized by her. How long can he resist the allure of her body?<br><br>Not long, but Alejandro Martinez doesn't do hearts and flowers, and everyone around him is in constant danger. Can Lexie deal with everything that comes with sharing "El Diablo's" bed?<br><br>Blood, passion and intense heartache will be something well known by Alejandro and Lexie. But their love is something indestructible, it will become their salvation, and their demise. <br><br>Since Alejandro is Briggs's uncle ( The heroine from Crave Me) all the characters from The Good 'Ol Boys series make an appearance, but this book is a complete standalone, is not necessary to read any previous books, to understand and enjoy this novel.<br><br>Reading <i>El Diablo</i> was an experience like no other. This anti-hero made me love him, and hate him with equal intensity. He owned my heart and haunted my dreams. He was an unapologetic villain, a dark angel, with a delicious hint of a latin flavor, and I wanted him to devour me. <br><br>Standing ovation to author M. Robinson for always delivering exactly what I want, and need, even if she has to rip my heart to shreds in the process. <br><br>If you are someone who enjoys passionate reads, with extreme angst, and are not afraid to get your heart shattered, <b>YOU MUST READ THIS BOOK!!!!!!</b><br><br>Peligroso, sensual, e inolvidable... <i>Dangerous, sensual, and unforgettable...</i><br><br>My <i>El Diablo</i> music playlist:<br>*Sympathy For The Devil by The Rolling Stones<br>*Any Other Name by Thomas Newman<br>*Broken-Hearted Girl by Beyonce<br>*Fighter by Christina Aguilera <br>*I Hate You, I love You by Gnash <br><br><a href="http://s1366.photobucket.com/user/DVFmontoya/media/17631979_zpsogt4rrvf.png.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1453830803i/17878407.png" alt=" photo 17631979_zpsogt4rrvf.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></span>

<div id="review_1743435192" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1743435192" />
    <a title="Elfina Renee" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/24309155-elfina-renee"><img alt="Elfina Renee" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1485189256p2/24309155.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1743435192?book_show_action=true">Aug 30, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Elfina Renee" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Elfina Renee" href="/user/show/24309155-elfina-renee">Elfina Renee</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/24309155-elfina-renee?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/24309155-elfina-renee?shelf=mafia-romance">mafia-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/24309155-elfina-renee?shelf=cartel">cartel</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1743435192" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8149616835493911632">Was a ten star read but regrettably could only give five!<br/><a href='http://s1096.photobucket.com/user/Christine_Dilley/media/10%20stars.png.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1466647658i/19503249._SX540_.png' alt=' photo 10 stars.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/>Diablo lived up to the hype and the well deserved reviews, comments, and gifs my Goodread’s friends raved about. Set in true cartel, mafia fashion. Alejandro played his villainous role as the devil perfectly! He was everything I embodied in an asshole. When I hated him, OMG I was ready to commit book murder. Yes there is such a thing. It's called chucking the tablet down and being very inventive over his death, nothing was off limits! </span>
  <span id="freeText8149616835493911632" style="display:none">Was a ten star read but regrettably could only give five!<br><a href="http://s1096.photobucket.com/user/Christine_Dilley/media/10%20stars.png.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1466647658i/19503249._SX540_.png" alt=" photo 10 stars.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>Diablo lived up to the hype and the well deserved reviews, comments, and gifs my Goodread’s friends raved about. Set in true cartel, mafia fashion. Alejandro played his villainous role as the devil perfectly! He was everything I embodied in an asshole. When I hated him, OMG I was ready to commit book murder. Yes there is such a thing. It's called chucking the tablet down and being very inventive over his death, nothing was off limits! I could practically hear the Godfather intro as the scenes vividly flashed in my head. <br><a href="http://s1096.photobucket.com/user/Christine_Dilley/media/Marcellos%20Legacy%2012.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1449083024ra/17231449.gif" alt=" photo Marcellos Legacy 12.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>The women in the novel were no whimpering violets, they were strong despite various circumstances, showing true grit. A few I wanted to throttle. You know never let a good crisis go to waste, kinda thing. Complex plot, unexpected twists and heat? Girl you better crank the AC up because your undies will practically melt right off.... scorching hot!<br><a href="http://s1096.photobucket.com/user/Christine_Dilley/media/BampB%2007.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1462548071i/19012642.jpg" alt=" photo BampB 07.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br></span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1771227988" />
    <a title="Karla" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10919114-karla"><img alt="Karla" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1596255037p2/10919114.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1771227988?book_show_action=true">Oct 02, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Karla" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Karla" href="/user/show/10919114-karla">Karla</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1771227988" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4826240809616866835">4.5 stars <br/><br/>At the risk of sounding like a broken record I'm gonna say again, this one blew me away!! Before I started reading it I was mentally preparing myself for the ride and plus I didn't read a lot of reviews just a couple.....but then I saw the word anti hero and I knew I had to read it. I Love anti heroes, even though they're kinda tricky because for me there has to be a good reason or explanation why, and a believable redemption of the anti hero. This one was absolutely fantastic Alejandr</span>
  <span id="freeText4826240809616866835" style="display:none">4.5 stars <br><br>At the risk of sounding like a broken record I'm gonna say again, this one blew me away!! Before I started reading it I was mentally preparing myself for the ride and plus I didn't read a lot of reviews just a couple.....but then I saw the word anti hero and I knew I had to read it. I Love anti heroes, even though they're kinda tricky because for me there has to be a good reason or explanation why, and a believable redemption of the anti hero. This one was absolutely fantastic Alejandro Martinez was the true definition of an AH. <br><br>"El Diablo" is the story of Alejandro and Lexi, this two were doom right from the start. It's told from dual POV and it starts when Alejandro, is about fifteen, his the son a powerful drug lord and right off the bat we know his destiny is to follow his father's foot steps. So we get to see Alejandro grow up to be a ruthless man just like his father but more importantly we see why, through his losses, that were so painful for him. Then we meet Lexi from when she's a little girl to when she meets Alejandro, I have to mention Alejandro is almost twice Lexi's age. But nothing happened between them till Lexi was a mature woman. So they meet a few times over the years till finally they come together. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1475477789ra/20724235.gif" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The relationship between this two was intense and yes, Alejandro, I'm not gonna lie was a huge jerk and was cruel with Lexi at times, never physically though. He would run hot and cold leaving me with chills, but regardless I loved this man. Knowing from the beginning what he went through helped me, so much to understand him, he was ruthless but so passionate and protective and so dam sexy. Lexi was a good match for him, she always felt an attraction to him, a connection. Coming from a bad childhood herself her only salvation had been her love of ballet dancing. She took a lot from Alejandro but I never thought of her as a weak h, I liked the she sassed him and fought for him. There sexual relationship was like foreplay, it wasn't insta it had a built up that it just made hotter, imo. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1475477789ra/20724236.gif" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This book was so fantastic I loved the writing, the story was fast paced, full of twists and turns. The last couple of chapters had my throat dry up, because I literally had my mouth fully open form shock!! <br>The only reason it didn't hit the five star was because the last time this two were separated was too long for me and I felt like there was character that really didn't need to be added, imo. But other than that I love it and the epilogue was perfect!<br> <br>"Te amo, cariño, por siempre" <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1475477789ra/20724237.gif" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>This was my first book by this author and I'm looking forward to reading the spinoff of this book with creed and Mia's story! &lt;3</span>
  <a data-text-id="4826240809616866835" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

How many bodies did he rack up on his journey to being one the most feared men of his time and who was the woman that brought him to his knees.<br/><br/> This was the story of how money,power, and a forbidden love became the ultimate demise of the one and only Alejandro Martinez.<br/><br/>Being the heir to a Drug Empire, Martin</span>
  <span id="freeText10760372619176303722" style="display:none">★★★★4 Diablo Stars★★★★<br><br><a href="http://s1148.photobucket.com/user/sannydmcmillans/media/Mobile%20Uploads/1472536915800_zps3ny3tdkk.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br>I have been practically chomping at the bit to read this story and like everyone else, I was wondering how did Alejandro Martinez become the infamous El Diablo? How many bodies did he rack up on his journey to being one the most feared men of his time and who was the woman that brought him to his knees.<br><br> This was the story of how money,power, and a forbidden love became the ultimate demise of the one and only Alejandro Martinez.<br><br>Being the heir to a Drug Empire, Martinez knew the rules of the game. His father was feared, and carrying on that tradition, he became the same way and so much more. He became powerful and well respected in his own right but make no mistake,if you cross him, certain body parts will be floating in the nearest river. They don't call him the devil for nothing and after reading this, I knew why. <br><br><a href="http://s1148.photobucket.com/user/sannydmcmillans/media/Mobile%20Uploads/1472534708985_zpskye1sx3y.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br>Lexi hasn't had a good childhood. Having a mother that was depressed and not being involved as much as she should, she learned from a very young age how to take care of herself as best as she could. But soon tragedy entered in her life and what little sense of normalcy she had, quickly became a thing of the past. But then she came face to face with the devil himself and her world was suddenly set on fire.<br><br><b> <i> "I'm in the business of making things go wrong. I'm not your prince charming, and once you realize that, it would make things alot easier."<br><br>On you? " <br><br>"No. You". I know who I am. It's you that doesn't".</i></b>  <br><br>I'm going to admit and say that Martinez tested my patience. As much as I LOVED him, I HATED some of his descisions with Lexi. Yes he took over the family bussiness but he made that Empire into what it was. Every deal, every hit, you knew it came from him and messing with the people he loved will only get you a closed casket. <br><br>But the moment you get a glimpse of his human side, you know that falling in love with a man like him might not be such a bad thing. I lived for those moments, I craved his love as much as Lexi did but I also craved his darkness. <br><br><a href="http://s1148.photobucket.com/user/sannydmcmillans/media/Mobile%20Uploads/tumblr_npaalhqyTP1uodbvyo1_500_zpskuzm1skx.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br>If you think you know what's going to happen, think again. The stomach turning twists and the heart palpating angst will have you in a battle of good vs evil. Martinez and Lexi's story is not one to be missed. <br><br><b>*Arc kindy provided I'm exchange for an honest review.</b></span>

<div id="review_1741911067" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1741911067" />
    <a title="Beverly" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13095060-beverly"><img alt="Beverly" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1466964369p2/13095060.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1741911067?book_show_action=true">Aug 28, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Beverly" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Beverly" href="/user/show/13095060-beverly">Beverly</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1741911067" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2060065747048471107">This book, I swear it’s something. Let me start by saying it was completely addictive, from the beginning I was intrigued and wanted to know Alejandro Martinez’s story. This man is insane, ruthless and dominating. He will stop at nothing to get what he wants, it’s that level of intensity that gave him the nickname, The Devil.<br/><br/>When we first meet Alejandro he is just a child and we see how this young boy turned into the monster he is now. I will be honest, there were so many times I was reading thi</span>
  <span id="freeText2060065747048471107" style="display:none">This book, I swear it’s something. Let me start by saying it was completely addictive, from the beginning I was intrigued and wanted to know Alejandro Martinez’s story. This man is insane, ruthless and dominating. He will stop at nothing to get what he wants, it’s that level of intensity that gave him the nickname, The Devil.<br><br>When we first meet Alejandro he is just a child and we see how this young boy turned into the monster he is now. I will be honest, there were so many times I was reading this story I actually felt for him. He was just an innocent child who was molded and manipulated by his father. Then he became El Diablo and my compassionate went out the window. It's hard to feel for this ruthless man. He owns every situation he is in and is feared by everyone. <br><br>We meet Lexi when she is a young girl too, but it’s years later when Alejandro is an adult because she is years younger than him. Lexi is a beautiful young girl who loves to ballet. Her mother suffers from depression and refuses to leave the house. She is a neglectful parent to Lexi, but Lexi loves her mother nonetheless. When her mother dies her life changes, too. She becomes a victim of abuse and spends years just trying to survive. <br><br>This story is really all about how little things completely change and shape these characters lives. Lexi and Alejandro meet when she is fifteen by random chance and neither forget each other. It’s years later before they run into each other again, but this connection is always present between them. I actually really liked Martinez and Lexi together. He was hard on her, but I understood is motivation. In the end, he just wanted to protect her and sometimes that meant pushing her away. <br><br>This story is crazy, crazy, crazy, crazy. It’s also pretty over the top. I swear that last 10% I was literally saying WTF out loud. It was crazy, but again it had me turning the page. This entire story is a page turner. It’s fast paced, angsty and dark. Their relationship is unexpected, but the connection and unwavering feelings are genuine. I don't think I will be forgetting these plot twists anytime soon!<br><br><b>
  <i>ARC kindly provided in exchange for an honest review. </i>

<div id="review_1670991147" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1670991147" />
    <a title="CC" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/12625026-cc"><img alt="CC" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1558473771p2/12625026.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1670991147?book_show_action=true">Jun 16, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="CC" class="user" itemprop="url" name="CC" href="/user/show/12625026-cc">CC</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12625026-cc?shelf=arc">arc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12625026-cc?shelf=action">action</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12625026-cc?shelf=oozing-sex-appeal">oozing-sex-appeal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12625026-cc?shelf=mafia-underworld-assassins">mafia-underworld-assassins</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1670991147" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4467422649412089551"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1472864191i/20331044._SY540_.jpg' width='400' height='420' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Alejandro Martinez was destined to fulfill the path already chosen for him leading to a life of crime, corruption, greed, lies and tragedy. At 20 years old, he was already feared and known as El Diablo, but knowing the destruction and pain his family caused, Alejandro vows to protect what remains in his life despite the consequences. Learning to be a “Martinez” at a very young age, Alejandro shields his heart but as decades pass, he begins to question whether loneliness is his fate or a fool’s c</span>
  <span id="freeText4467422649412089551" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1472864191i/20331044._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="420" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Alejandro Martinez was destined to fulfill the path already chosen for him leading to a life of crime, corruption, greed, lies and tragedy. At 20 years old, he was already feared and known as El Diablo, but knowing the destruction and pain his family caused, Alejandro vows to protect what remains in his life despite the consequences. Learning to be a “Martinez” at a very young age, Alejandro shields his heart but as decades pass, he begins to question whether loneliness is his fate or a fool’s choice. <br><br><b>
  <blockquote> “This is what we do, hijo. We protect what’s ours any means necessary. No. Matter. What. Family comes first.” </blockquote>
</b><br>Having a childhood marred by neglect, Lexi learned at a young age to fend for herself and to take joy in the art of ballet. In trying to be independent and follow her dream, Lexi applies for a job at an establishment owned by Martinez. Exuding his influence in subtle ways, Alejandro cannot turn his back on Lexi. After feeling a strong connection with Alejandro, the tension builds but neither could have imagined how their futures would blend in so many ways. <br><br><b>
  <blockquote> “I want you to come on my fingers, cariño, I want to see your face get flushed, your breathing hitch. I want to feel your pussy pulsate so fucking hard it pushes my fingers out of your sweet little hole.” </blockquote>
</b><br>As Alejandro is a conflicted man suffering an incredible amount of despair, he steadfastly forges ahead to lead the Martinez family legacy. After vowing to never open his heart to anyone again, Lexi tests Alejandro, and while it’s his nature to protect and love, he can’t give what he wants despite her wholehearted acceptance of Alejandro’s dual personas.<br> <br><b>
  <blockquote> “I warned you. I told you I don’t know how to love. I ordered you to stay away from me, time and time again. I’m not the man you think I am. I never was.” </blockquote>
</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1472625483ra/20216403.gif" width="400" height="220" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <blockquote> “The good and bad. Heaven and hell. Every part of him. I took what I could get. Every last ounce of him.” </blockquote>
</b><br>Alejandro is a man of deep passion whether he is showing his gentle or vile side and I like how he wavered between these warring factions within himself. The tender moments were so warm which served to reinforce his true nature because if he was as ruthless as his father, Alejandro would have been a very different man. By the end, I felt comfortable with his choice of possible salvation with Lexi but parts of “the how” didn’t seem to completely coalesce with his character. However, it didn’t deter from the impact of Alejandro’s journey and the arc of his character development. <br><br>As for Lexi, I admired her resilience and ability to balance the positive and negative in her life. By choosing Alejandro and his lifestyle, Lexi was fully aware of the risks involved yet she was willing take a chance whether it lasted for a brief moment or for more time than she could imagine. To me, Lexi proved she was a match for Alejandro.<br><br>Also, the secondary characters were vital to supporting the failures and successes of the main characters and the ongoing plot. For those familiar with the The Good Ol’ Boys series, being reunited with some friendly faces will be an added plus. I would like to know more about Alejandro’s friend, Leo, in the future. <br><br>From the onset of El Diablo, an epic tone is cast upon the Martinez family that unfolds into a richly developed plot spanning many years and a multitude of dimensional characters. With engaging prose, M. Robinson successfully captures a story steeped love, violence, passion, redemption and friendship. I highly recommend! <br><br><br><br><br><i>*An ARC was generously provided by the author in exchange for an honest review.<br><br><br>* This was a (F)BR with Hawkey, Liz, Loyda and Sue! *<br></i></span>
  <a data-text-id="4467422649412089551" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer13410420923060957021"><b>*** 3.5 Stars ***</b><br/><br/>WHOA. That was an angstfest. <br/>Utterly addicting. <br/>Definitely a book for dark readers who love an anti-hero. <br/><br/>I would also say, CONTENT warning: <a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view spoiler)</a><span class='spoilerContainer' style='display: none'>[violence, rape, lots of dark thing happening here.  <a class='jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction'>(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> Shocking stuff.... hahahaha! <br/><br/>I'm still trying to sort my thoughts.   <span id="freeText13410420923060957021" style="display:none"><b>*** 3.5 Stars ***</b><br /><br />WHOA. That was an angstfest. <br />Utterly addicting. <br />Definitely a book for dark readers who love an anti-hero. <br /><br />I would also say, CONTENT warning: <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[violence, rape, lots of dark thing happening here.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> Shocking stuff.... hahahaha! <br /><br />I'm still trying to sort my thoughts. I don't really know how I feel. I just.. IDK. I hated Martinez. And just when I thought I could like him, he ruined it for me. While I could sympathize with his plight, I couldn't connect to his crazy. He just ... IDK. And that twist, I can't get over it. Hahahahaha! I JUST CAN'T GET OVER IT. WHOA! <br /><br />One thing I will say is that no matter how many times I put it down, no matter how many times I said, enough, I can't handle this man anymore, I kept reading. I want to stand up and applaud M. Robinson for gut punching me repeatedly. Addicting for sure. <br /><br />I would absolutely recommend this book to the people who LOVE a dark book. </span>

    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1873367841" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16818483439033028229"><b>4 Rollercoaster Stars<br/>* * * * <br/>Keeping this short as so many others have done terrific reviews of this book... so good, it caused me to take the time to read it. </b><br/><br/>This is not for the faint of heart...It is exactly what is advertised...Ruthless behavior happening throughout the book. A crime family so destructive, no one is safe from its clutches. <br/><br/>Father corrupts son...<br/>Sister fears with good reason what her brother is turning into...<br/>A young man destroyed by his destiny and must learn how to survive </span>
  <span id="freeText16818483439033028229" style="display:none"><b>4 Rollercoaster Stars<br>* * * * <br>Keeping this short as so many others have done terrific reviews of this book... so good, it caused me to take the time to read it. </b><br><br>This is not for the faint of heart...It is exactly what is advertised...Ruthless behavior happening throughout the book. A crime family so destructive, no one is safe from its clutches. <br><br>Father corrupts son...<br>Sister fears with good reason what her brother is turning into...<br>A young man destroyed by his destiny and must learn how to survive and conquer it all...<br>or be eaten alive...<br><br>A girl taught from the start, life is unfair...<br>The beauty of ballet and the music her only escape...<br><br>These two cross paths.. and we ride through the decades of want, guilt, deceit, truths cloaked in lies and love... undying love...sometimes misguided...<br><br>An all-encompassing tale with a man who can be a savior and the devil himself. A woman who didn't flinch and turn her back on him...<br>Even when she should.<br><br>I enjoyed this for the most part..there was a point where it felt long but then picked up again in the end. This is a stand-alone, however there were enough hints about other characters from this to know another book will be coming. Worth the read. <br><br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/30201299.El_Diablo__The_Devil___1_" title="El Diablo (The Devil, #1) by M. Robinson" rel="nofollow noopener">

  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/books/1595607124l/43093216._SY75_.jpg" alt="El Diablo II by M. Robinson" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> El Diablo II (The Devil, #2)<br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3530326586">https://www.goodreads.com/review/show...</a><br> <br><b>~~~~~ Before Reading ~~~~~</b><br><b>

  <span id="freeText17963101941524840740" style="display:none"><a href="http://s1260.photobucket.com/user/linalove1988/media/newreviewbannerfeather_zpspga5dbag.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a> <br><br><br><br><br><i>{ARC kindly provided by M. Robinson in exchange for an honest review.}</i><br><br><br><a href="http://s1260.photobucket.com/user/linalove1988/media/rosebuttonsmall_zpsrpi6fijr.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1458381064i/18481158.jpg" alt=" photo rosebuttonsmall_zpsrpi6fijr.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="http://s1260.photobucket.com/user/linalove1988/media/rosebuttonsmall_zpsrpi6fijr.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1458381064i/18481158.jpg" alt=" photo rosebuttonsmall_zpsrpi6fijr.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="http://s1260.photobucket.com/user/linalove1988/media/rosebuttonsmall_zpsrpi6fijr.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1458381064i/18481158.jpg" alt=" photo rosebuttonsmall_zpsrpi6fijr.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <br><br><b>Title:</b> El Diablo<br><b>Author:</b> M. Robinson<br><b>Category:</b> Mafia, Romance<br><b>Series or Standalone:</b> Standalone<br><b>POV:</b> Dual<br><b>Plot:</b> 5<br><b>Characters:</b> 5<br><b>Scorching Level:</b> 5<br><b>HEA:</b> Not telling<br><br>Jesus Christ! I feel like my heart was put through the grinder!!! What an amazing story.<br>M. Robinson has outdone herself with this book. The raw emotions, the heart-breaking twists and turns made this book a masterpiece. There is pain, danger, love, passion, fear and torment. <br>The author puts her characters through hell but they come out stronger than before, vibrating with life and determination.<br>The book is very intricate and in its essence it is a story about love and family. The storyline is built slowly and executed in utter perfection. The characters grow as the years pass and I loved how she developed the various storylines.<br>The book is about Alejandro Martinez, the son of a very powerful Colombian crime lord. The book has the feeling of an autobiography in the sense that we get to experience the feelings first hand from the hero's point of view. We get to meet the innocent Alejandro, the one with hopes and aspirations for a better future and then watch him transform into the man his father always wanted. We get to see his loss and pain as he grows up to become the one and only El Diablo.<br>Alone and ruthlessly determined to fulfill his destiny, he becomes cold and detached to anything and everyone that can be seen as a weakness. <br>We see him turn his back on love but can he survive without it?<br>I will not get into plot details because the book must be experienced without any knowledge but know this; the author has created one of her best heroes ever. Alejandro Martinez is a complex and multi-dimensional man who fights with who he is every second of his life. He is and breathes hell but he is not a demon. This man's journey will stay with me forever and this book is one of my favorites. <br>Do yourself a favor and do not miss this masterpiece. I highly recommend this. Let <i>El Diablo</i> take you on a journey that you won't ever forget. <br><br>5 Devilish Stars! I would give it more if I could.<br><br><br><br><br><a href="http://s1260.photobucket.com/user/linalove1988/media/newbanner2_zpsjiptvrlr.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1454329607i/17945482._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo newbanner2_zpsjiptvrlr.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

<div id="review_1745311563" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1745311563" />
    <a title="BleuBelle" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/21818379-bleubelle"><img alt="BleuBelle" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1604586298p2/21818379.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1745311563?book_show_action=true">Sep 01, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="BleuBelle" class="user" itemprop="url" name="BleuBelle" href="/user/show/21818379-bleubelle">BleuBelle</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/21818379-bleubelle?shelf=disappointed">disappointed</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/21818379-bleubelle?shelf=hea">hea</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/21818379-bleubelle?shelf=hero-older-than-her">hero-older-than-her</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/21818379-bleubelle?shelf=not-my-style">not-my-style</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/21818379-bleubelle?shelf=emotional">emotional</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/21818379-bleubelle?shelf=man-whore">man-whore</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/21818379-bleubelle?shelf=cheater">cheater</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/21818379-bleubelle?shelf=horrible">horrible</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/21818379-bleubelle?shelf=hate-the-hero">hate-the-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/21818379-bleubelle?shelf=pushy-hero">pushy-hero</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1745311563" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16443667567478210607">If I've had the energy to write an review I would. But I don't. Reading this story totally left me with nothing. I have so many things to say about this book, but that would fill out pages. So I'm not going to do it.<br/><br/>The important things are: I HATE this book. I was really disappointed. The Hero isn't hero-worthy. Too many bad things are happening in this book. HEA was there but I didn't read it to the end, because I had no interest AT ALL. Lexi and Alejandro can do what they want, don't want to </span>
  <span id="freeText16443667567478210607" style="display:none">If I've had the energy to write an review I would. But I don't. Reading this story totally left me with nothing. I have so many things to say about this book, but that would fill out pages. So I'm not going to do it.<br /><br />The important things are: I HATE this book. I was really disappointed. The Hero isn't hero-worthy. Too many bad things are happening in this book. HEA was there but I didn't read it to the end, because I had no interest AT ALL. Lexi and Alejandro can do what they want, don't want to know!!<br /><br />Hero is an asshole. He's hurting everyone he loves. And why? Because he thinks he's "protecting" them. He's a cheater. A coward. Immature. He breaks Lexis heart over and over and over again. So many times, I can't count. He cheated. He has sex with other women, the same night Lexi was nearly raped (Lexie hears all of it, because he takes the one-night-stand home and his room is right next to Lexis). He's going hot and cold all the time. I wouldn't know where his feelings are. That's emotional abuse for me. Because he wont let Lexi go. The first time they have sex (Lexi is a virgin and has history of abuse) he treated her like a whore. His words! Lexi didn't deserve any of this.<br /><br />Heroine was ok. I really liked her. But I wanted to shake some sense into her, because she let the hero walk all over her. She was giving and trying and forgiving. And what did he do? Not one damn thing.<br /><br />The scene near the end where Lexi goes back to his apartment after finding all this tabloids with other women? And then finding Alejandro in bed with another women? I felt sick. Because I could hear my heart breaking for Lexi. I never felt so disgusted while reading a book.<br /><br />The ending? Well... Alejandro explains all his actions to Lexi. He wants her forgiveness. Here's the first time he apologizes and tells her he loves her. But for me it was a too little too late. But I'm not Lexi (thank God). Then there is a 3 month separation and Lexi goes back to him with ultimatums. Because she's pregnant with his daughter. And what does Alejandro do? Decides that now that she's pregnant with his baby and didn't tell him before (because she thought he was dead), she has to be with him even if she wouldn't want it. And to hell with the ultimatums. He doesn't care about that. He just wants to f*** her.<br /><br />So I skipped the epilogue. Don't want to know.<br /><br />This seems really harsh, but that's how I feel about the book. I just wanted a hero whom I could believe in. He doesn't has to be perfect, far from it. But he should have some "swoon" worthy points. And I didn't get to experience this with Alejandro. Not one time!</span>
  <a data-text-id="16443667567478210607" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer1746304483" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11625210016922040201"><br/>My short review would be it is : A very, very and I mean VERY long and pointless book !! <br/> (warning double exclamation points galore to convey my irritable mood after reading this) <br/>I cannot fathom how anyone would think this rambling story was any good. I don't know this "M. Robinson" but I sure as hell haven't read anything so lukewarm and dull in a long time !!<br/><br/>There are 40 plus chapters of utter bullsh*t between the MC, the supposedly hero & heroine don't even meet until chapter twenty somethin</span>
  <span id="freeText11625210016922040201" style="display:none"><br />My short review would be it is : A very, very and I mean VERY long and pointless book !! <br /> (warning double exclamation points galore to convey my irritable mood after reading this) <br />I cannot fathom how anyone would think this rambling story was any good. I don't know this "M. Robinson" but I sure as hell haven't read anything so lukewarm and dull in a long time !!<br /><br />There are 40 plus chapters of utter bullsh*t between the MC, the supposedly hero &amp; heroine don't even meet until chapter twenty something. Instead we can read about the "hero" sad family story and first love interest who turns out to be the heroine's mother #facepalm<br /><br /> Did I mention the huge ellipses in time which span from 3 to 10 years separation ? There is also a little flaw in the book structure: NO PLOT anywhere. <br /><br />To recap :the main characters are spineless idiots who need therapy, so I'd recommend you Do not believe the hype. Please don't buy into the angsty dark romance blurb because you'll lose money and time on this flimsy idea of a romance !!</span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1806658318" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16866060890584809414">DNF @57%<br/><br/>This was boring. The story moved sooooooooo slowly. I expected the hero to be dangerous, dark, and ruthless, but instead I got a melancholy moping man whose whining self-pity went on and on. He's too weak for my liking.<br/><br/>I can't say much about the heroine because she'd just appeared in the story at around 40% of the book. Much as I wanted to know more about her, I couldn't hold on anymore. This one wasn't for me.<br/><br/>I'm sorry.<br/></span>

          </span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('Vs0qYHNc6vWN8+StTnakRKlMMPsSrcHmMsyrJXhC/lTwqB/q2zjORr5WmHWIjiVibLAjRPh2eO4SnGK68/GfGg==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('PPn+snTtywm7r/6FuNgsCrrXGM532iAIGsSW2rlasv2anMs43InvuogKgl1+IK0sfysLcZ0BmQA6lF9FMunTsw==')})
  }
//]]>

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer4734625058969136553">M. Robinson is the Wall Street Journal & USA Today Bestselling Author crowned as the “Queen of Angst” by readers around the world. Dive into her visionary world that will take you on a rollercoaster ride of emotions and leave you wanting more. She writes everything from contemporary to suspense romance and is best known for her novel, El Diablo.<br/><br/>When M isn’t in the cave writing her next epic love s</span>
  <span id="freeText4734625058969136553" style="display:none">M. Robinson is the Wall Street Journal &amp; USA Today Bestselling Author crowned as the “Queen of Angst” by readers around the world. Dive into her visionary world that will take you on a rollercoaster ride of emotions and leave you wanting more. She writes everything from contemporary to suspense romance and is best known for her novel, El Diablo.<br /><br />When M isn’t in the cave writing her next epic love story, you will find her shopping and living on a boat in Florida with her real life pirate, her lobster, her husband Bossman. Sipping on Starbucks and hanging out with their two dogs, a German shepherd mix and a gordito Wheaten Terrier reading a good book. Or spending time with her family, who she is extremely close with. <br /><br />Above all, M loves her readers more than anything and loves to connect with them! She is on all social media platforms @authormrobinson but you will find her in her happy place the most. Her VIP Reader Group on Facebook or her second favorite happy place, Instagram. <br /><br />Stay connected!</span>
